[t7].[AddressTypeCode], [t7].[AddressTypeName], [t7].[CreatedBy4], [t7].[DateCreated4], [t7].[DateUpdated4], [t7].[LastUpdatedBy4]
FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[FirstName], [p].[LastName], [p].[Email], [p].[PhoneNumber], [p].[PersonsDob], [p].[NationalId], [e].[EquityDesc], [d].[DisabilityStatusDesc], [h].[HomeLanguageDesc], [c].[CitizenshipStatusDesc], [n].[NationalityDesc], [g].[GenderDesc], [p].[PhotoName], [p].[PhotoPath], [p].[Id], [c].[CitizenshipStatusId], [g].[GenderId]
    FROM [Person] AS [p]
    LEFT JOIN [Equity] AS [e] ON [p].[EquityId] = [e].[EquityId]
    LEFT JOIN [DisabilityStatus] AS [d] ON [p].[DisabilityStatusId] = [d].[DisabilityStatusId]
    LEFT JOIN [HomeLanguage] AS [h] ON [p].[HomeLanguageId] = [h].[HomeLanguageId]
    INNER JOIN [CitizenshipStatus] AS [c] ON [p].[CitizenshipStatusId] = [c].[CitizenshipStatusId]
    LEFT JOIN [Nationality] AS [n] ON [p].[NationalityId] = [n].[NationalityId]
    INNER JOIN [Gender] AS [g] ON [p].[GenderId] = [g].[GenderId]
    WHERE [p].[Email] = @__email_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [a].[AddressId], [a].[AddressTypeId], [a].[CityId], [a].[CompanyId], [a].[CountryId], [a].[CreatedBy], [a].[DateCreated], [a].[DateUpdated], [a].[HouseNo], [a].[LastUpdatedBy], [a].[PersonId], [a].[PostalCode], [a].[ProvinceId], [a].[StreetName], [a].[SuburbId], [c0].[CountryId] AS [CountryId0], [c0].[CountryCode], [c0].[CountryName], [c0].[CreatedBy] AS [CreatedBy0], [c0].[DateCreated] AS [DateCreated0], [c0].[DateUpdated] AS [DateUpdated0], [c0].[LastUpdatedBy] AS [LastUpdatedBy0], [c1].[CityId] AS [CityId0], [c1].[CityCode], [c1].[CityName], [c1].[CreatedBy] AS [CreatedBy1], [c1].[DateCreated] AS [DateCreated1], [c1].[DateUpdated] AS [DateUpdated1], [c1].[LastUpdatedBy] AS [LastUpdatedBy1], [c1].[ProvinceId] AS [ProvinceId0], [s].[SuburbId] AS [SuburbId0], [s].[CityId] AS [CityId1], [s].[CreatedBy] AS [CreatedBy2], [s].[DateCreated] AS [DateCreated2], [s].[DateUpdated] AS [DateUpdated2], [s].[LastUpdatedBy] AS [LastUpdatedBy2], [s].[SuburbCode], [s].[SuburbName], [p0].[ProvinceId] AS [ProvinceId1], [p0].[CountryId] AS [CountryId1], [p0].[CreatedBy] AS [CreatedBy3], [p0].[DateCreated] AS [DateCreated3], [p0].[DateUpdated] AS [DateUpdated3], [p0].[LastUpdatedBy] AS [LastUpdatedBy3], [p0].[ProvinceCode], [p0].[ProvinceName], [a0].[AddressTypeId] AS [AddressTypeId0], [a0].[AddressTypeCode], [a0].[AddressTypeName], [a0].[CreatedBy] AS [CreatedBy4], [a0].[DateCreated] AS [DateCreated4], [a0].[DateUpdated] AS [DateUpdated4], [a0].[LastUpdatedBy] AS [LastUpdatedBy4]
    FROM [Address] AS [a]
    LEFT JOIN [Country] AS [c0] ON [a].[CountryId] = [c0].[CountryId]
    LEFT JOIN [City] AS [c1] ON [a].[CityId] = [c1].[CityId]
    LEFT JOIN [Suburb] AS [s] ON [a].[SuburbId] = [s].[SuburbId]
    LEFT JOIN [Province] AS [p0] ON [a].[ProvinceId] = [p0].[ProvinceId]
    LEFT JOIN [AddressType] AS [a0] ON [a].[AddressTypeId] = [a0].[AddressTypeId]

    LEFT JOIN [DisabilityStatus] AS [d] ON [p].[DisabilityStatusId] = [d].[DisabilityStatusId]
    LEFT JOIN [HomeLanguage] AS [h] ON [p].[HomeLanguageId] = [h].[HomeLanguageId]

[t7].[AddressTypeCode], [t7].[AddressTypeName], [t7].[CreatedBy4], [t7].[DateCreated4], [t7].[DateUpdated4], [t7].[LastUpdatedBy4]
FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[FirstName], [p].[LastName], [p].[Email], [p].[PhoneNumber], [p].[PersonsDob], [p].[NationalId], [e].[EquityDesc], [d].[DisabilityStatusDesc], [h].[HomeLanguageDesc], [c].[CitizenshipStatusDesc], [n].[NationalityDesc], [g].[GenderDesc], [p].[PhotoName], [p].[PhotoPath], [p].[Id], [c].[CitizenshipStatusId], [g].[GenderId]
    FROM [Person] AS [p]
    LEFT JOIN [Equity] AS [e] ON [p].[EquityId] = [e].[EquityId]
    LEFT JOIN [DisabilityStatus] AS [d] ON [p].[DisabilityStatusId] = [d].[DisabilityStatusId]
    LEFT JOIN [HomeLanguage] AS [h] ON [p].[HomeLanguageId] = [h].[HomeLanguageId]
    INNER JOIN [CitizenshipStatus] AS [c] ON [p].[CitizenshipStatusId] = [c].[CitizenshipStatusId]
    LEFT JOIN [Nationality] AS [n] ON [p].[NationalityId] = [n].[NationalityId]
    INNER JOIN [Gender] AS [g] ON [p].[GenderId] = [g].[GenderId]
    WHERE [p].[Email] = @__email_0

[t7].[AddressTypeCode], [t7].[AddressTypeName], [t7].[CreatedBy4], [t7].[DateCreated4], [t7].[DateUpdated4], [t7].[LastUpdatedBy4]
FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[FirstName], [p].[LastName], [p].[Email], [p].[PhoneNumber], [p].[PersonsDob], [p].[NationalId], [e].[EquityDesc], [d].[DisabilityStatusDesc], [h].[HomeLanguageDesc], [c].[CitizenshipStatusDesc], [n].[NationalityDesc], [g].[GenderDesc], [p].[PhotoName], [p].[PhotoPath], [p].[Id], [c].[CitizenshipStatusId], [g].[GenderId]
    FROM [Person] AS [p]
    LEFT JOIN [Equity] AS [e] ON [p].[EquityId] = [e].[EquityId]
    LEFT JOIN [DisabilityStatus] AS [d] ON [p].[DisabilityStatusId] = [d].[DisabilityStatusId]
    LEFT JOIN [HomeLanguage] AS [h] ON [p].[HomeLanguageId] = [h].[HomeLanguageId]
    INNER JOIN [CitizenshipStatus] AS [c] ON [p].[CitizenshipStatusId] = [c].[CitizenshipStatusId]
    LEFT JOIN [Nationality] AS [n] ON [p].[NationalityId] = [n].[NationalityId]
    INNER JOIN [Gender] AS [g] ON [p].[GenderId] = [g].[GenderId]
    WHERE [p].[Email] = @__email_0
